    // (undocumented)

    // (undocumented)

    // (undocumented)

    // (undocumented)

    text?: React_2.ReactNode;
    // (undocumented)

    // (undocumented)
    type?: 'button' | 'reset' | 'submit';
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface PopoverProps extends ResponsiveRadiusProps, ResponsiveShadowProps, ResponsiveWidthProps {
    // (undocumented)
    allowedAutoPlacements?: Placement[];
    // (undocumented)
    arrow?: boolean;
    // (undocumented)
    boundaryElement?: HTMLElement | null;
    // (undocumented)
    children?: React_2.ReactElement;
    // (undocumented)
    constrainSize?: boolean;
    // (undocumented)
    content?: React_2.ReactNode;
    // (undocumented)
    disabled?: boolean;
    // (undocumented)
    fallbackPlacements?: Placement[];
    // (undocumented)
    open?: boolean;
    // (undocumented)

}

    // (undocumented)
    muted: ThemeColorMuted;

    solid: ThemeColorSolid;

    //
    // (undocumented)
    syntax: ThemeColorSyntax;
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface ThemeColorBase {
    // (undocumented)
    bg: string;
    // (undocumented)
    border: string;
    // (undocumented)
    fg: string;
    // (undocumented)
    focusRing: string;
    // (undocumented)
    shadow: {
        outline: string;
        umbra: string;
        penumbra: string;
        ambient: string;
    };
}

// @public (undocumented)
export interface ThemeColorBuilderOpts {
    // (undocumented)
    base: (opts: {
        dark: boolean;
        name: ThemeColorName;
    }) => ThemeColorBase;
    // (undocumented)
    button: (opts: {
        dark: boolean;
        mode: ThemeColorButtonModeKey;
        base: ThemeColorBase;
        solid: ThemeColorSolidTone;
        muted: ThemeColorMutedTone;
    }) => ThemeColorButtonStates;
    // (undocumented)
    card: (opts: {
        base: ThemeColorBase;
        dark: boolean;
        muted: ThemeColorMutedTone;
        name: ThemeColorName;
        solid: ThemeColorSolidTone;
        state: 'enabled' | 'disabled' | 'hovered' | 'pressed' | 'selected';
    }) => ThemeColorCardState;
    // (undocumented)
    input: (opts: {
        base: ThemeColorBase;
        solid: ThemeColorSolidTone;
        muted: ThemeColorMutedTone;
        dark: boolean;
        mode: 'default' | 'invalid';
        state: 'enabled' | 'disabled' | 'hovered';
    }) => ThemeColorInputState;
    // (undocumented)
    muted: (opts: {
        base: ThemeColorBase;
        dark: boolean;
        tone: ThemeColorToneKey;
        name: ThemeColorName;
        state: 'enabled' | 'disabled' | 'hovered' | 'pressed' | 'selected';
    }) => ThemeColorGenericState;
    // (undocumented)
    solid: (opts: {
        base: ThemeColorBase;
        dark: boolean;
        tone: ThemeColorToneKey;
        name: ThemeColorName;
        state: 'enabled' | 'disabled' | 'hovered' | 'pressed' | 'selected';
    }) => ThemeColorGenericState;
    // (undocumented)
    spot: (opts: {
        base: ThemeColorBase;
        dark: boolean;
        key: ThemeColorSpotKey;
    }) => string;
    // (undocumented)
    syntax: (opts: {
        base: ThemeColorBase;
        dark: boolean;
    }) => ThemeColorSyntax;
}
